Load packages, scripts and data

library(dplyr)

library(cmdstanr)
#> CmdStan path set to: /usr/share/cmdstan/cmdstan-2.36.0
#> This is cmdstanr version 0.9.0
#> - CmdStanR documentation and vignettes: mc-stan.org/cmdstanr

path_proj <- here::here()
path_src <- file.path(path_proj, "src")
path_models <- file.path(path_src, "models")
path_data <- file.path(path_proj, "data")
path_processed <- file.path(path_data, "processed")
path_modelled <- file.path(path_data, "modelled")
path_samples_huso <- file.path(path_data, "draws", "huso")

source(file.path(path_src, "20-processing.R"))
source(file.path(path_src, "30-eda.R"))
source(file.path(path_src, "50-modelling.R"))

huso <- readRDS(file.path(path_processed, "huso104_20110512_20110606.rds"))
range(huso$date)
#> [1] "2011-05-12" "2011-06-06"

Load and compile models

model_names <- c("nonparam", "gom", "gom_rw1", "gom_ou")
models <- file.path(path_models, paste0(model_names, ".stan")) |>
    lapply(cmdstan_model) |>
    setNames(model_names)

Fit models

Evaluate the priors for the cumulative reporting probability curves.

hypers <- hypers_q(phi_ref = 0.1, D_ref = 15, type = "gompertz", alpha_phi = 1.4, sd_log_b = 0.5, delay_seq = 0:15)

hypers
#> $alpha_phi
#> [1] 1.4
#> 
#> $beta_phi
#> [1] 9.933333
#> 
#> $mean_log_b
#> [1] -1.371937
#> 
#> $sd_log_b
#> [1] 0.5
#> 
#> $mean_logit_phi
#> [1] -2.306101
#> 
#> $sd_logit_phi
#> [1] 1.063609

Obtain mcmc samples for selected models assuming different ending times.

D <- 15
end_dates <- seq(as.Date("2011-05-25"), as.Date("2011-06-06"), by = "3 days")
samples_list <- nowcast_sample_dates(huso, models, hypers, end_dates, D,
    iter_sampling = 10000, iter_warmup = 5000, chains = 3,
    output_dir = path_samples_huso)
